- `-0.896123622766678*v`
- `-1.29395390256765*x*0.0943056786339846*Abs(v)**(1/3)` = `-0.12203...*x*Abs(v)**(1/3)`
- `-1.29395390256765*x` (from the `(... + 1)` part)
- `-1.29395390256765*x` (the separate term)
- `-0.448061811383339*sin(v)`

So GT = `c_a*x**3 + c_b*v + c_c*x + c_d*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) + c_e*sin(v)`

where the x term combines: `-1.29395390256765*x - 1.29395390256765*x = -2.5879...*x`

**GT basis functions:** `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), sin(v)}`

Now I'll check each candidate for whether it can express exactly these basis functions.

Key observations:
- `cos(c*v + c') = cos(c')*cos(c*v) - sin(c')*sin(c*v)`. Setting c5=1, c6=-π/2 gives `sin(v)`. So `c4*cos(c5*v + c6)` can produce `sin(v)`.
- `c1*sin(c2*v + c3)` with c2=1 gives `sin(v+c3) = sin(v)cos(c3) + cos(v)sin(c3)`. Setting c3=0 gives `sin(v)`.
- Extra terms with `t` cannot be zeroed unless their coefficient can be set to 0.

Let me systematically check each candidate:

**Candidate 1:** `c0*x**3 + c1*v + c2*x + c3*x*Abs(v)**(1/3) + c4*cos(c5*v + c6) + c7*cos(c8*t + c9)` — Has `cos(c8*t + c9)` which is t-dependent. Set c7=0. Then remaining: `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), cos(c5*v+c6)}` → cos can become sin(v). **MATCH**

**Candidate 2:** `... + c3*t**c4` — t-dependent term. Set c3=0. Remaining matches GT basis. **MATCH**

**Candidate 3:** `... + c4*exp(c5*t)` — Set c4=0. Remaining matches. **MATCH**

**Candidate 4:** `... + c7*t*(c8+x)**c9` — Set c7=0. Remaining matches. **MATCH**

**Candidate 5:** `... + c2 + ... + c8*t` — Set c2=0, c8=0. Remaining: `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), cos(c6*v+c7)}`. **MATCH**

**Candidate 6:** `... + c4*log(c5*t+1)` — Set c4=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 7:** `... + c7*t*(c8+v)**c9` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 8:** `... + c1*v**3 + c2*v**5 + ... + c6*sin(c7*v+c8)*cos(c9*t)` — The sin*cos(t) term: can't separate. Set c6=0, but then no sin(v) term remains. Also c1*v**3 and c2*v**5 are extra; set c1=c2=0. But then no sin(v). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 9:** `... + c2*sin(c3*t+c4)` — t-dependent. Set c2=0. Remaining has `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), cos(c8*v+c9)}`. **MATCH**

**Candidate 10:** `... + c3*x**c4` — If c4=1, this merges with x term. Remaining: `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), cos}`. **MATCH**

**Candidate 11:** `... + c3*v**c4` — If c4=1, merges with v. **MATCH**

**Candidate 12:** `... + c7*x*sin(c8*t+c9)` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 13:** `... + c7*x*cos(c8*t)` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 14:** `... + c1*v**3 + ... + c8*x*cos(c9*t)` — Set c1=0, c8=0. Has sin(c3*v+c4). **MATCH**

**Candidate 15:** `... + c7*v*cos(c8*t)` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 16:** `... + c3*exp(c4*x)` — Set c3=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 17:** `... + c2*sin(c3*v+c4) + ... + c7*cos(c8*v+c9)` — Both trig terms. Can produce sin(v) from either. Set one to give sin(v), other to 0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 18:** `... + c7*Max(0,x)**(3/2)` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 19:** `... + c1*v**3 + ... + x/(c8+t)**5` — The last term has coefficient 1 (not free). Can't zero it. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 20:** `... + x/(c7+t)**5` — Same issue, coefficient is 1. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 21:** `... + c8*x/(c9+t)**5` — Set c8=0. Set c1=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 22:** `... + c2*sin(c3*x+c4)` — sin of x, not v. Set c2=0. Then need sin(v) from cos(c8*v+c9). **MATCH**

**Candidate 23:** `... + c7*x/(c8+t)**5` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 24:** `... + c1*v**3 + ... + c7*log(c8*v+1)` — log(c8*v+1) is not equivalent to sin(v). Set c1=0, c7=0. But then no sin(v) term. Has sin(c3*v+c4) though! Set c1=0, c7=0. Remaining: `{x**3, sin(v), v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3)}`. **MATCH**

**Candidate 25:** `... + c1*x**2 + ... + c5*v**3` — Set c1=0, c5=0. Has sin(c3*v+c4). **MATCH**

**Candidate 26:** `... + c4*log(c5*x+1)` — Set c4=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 27:** `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), cos(c6*v+c7)} + c2` — Set c2=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 28:** Same as 27 with c8=0, c7 merges with c2. **MATCH**

**Candidate 29:** c1*v + c2*v = (c1+c2)*v, c3=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 30:** `... + c4*log(c5*v+1)` — v takes negative values, log undefined. Set c4=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 31:** `... + c4*exp(c5*v)` — Set c4=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 32:** `... + c7*x**c8*log(c9*Abs(v)+1)` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 33:** `c1*v**3 + ... + c5*v**5` — No cos/sin of v. Set c1=c5=0. No sin(v) term left. **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 34:** Has cos and v**3. Set c2=0. c1*v + c8*v combine. **MATCH**

**Candidate 35:** No cos term, only sin. Set c4=0. Has sin(c2*v+c3). **MATCH**

**Candidate 36:** Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 37:** `... + c7*x**5` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 38:** `{x**3, sin(c2*v+c3), v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3)}` — Exactly GT basis. **MATCH**

**Candidate 39:** Exactly `{x**3, v, x, x*Abs(v)**(1/3), cos(c5*v+c6)}`. **MATCH**

**Candidate 40:** c1*v + c7*v combine. **MATCH**

**Candidate 41:** `c2*v*x**2` — Set c2=0. c1*v + c8*v combine. **MATCH**

**Candidate 42:** Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 43:** `c7*v*Abs(v)` — Set c7=0. Has sin. **MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** `c7*v*Abs(v)` — Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 45:** `c6*exp(c7*t)*sin(...)` — Set c6=0. Then no sin(v). c1*v**3, c5*v*Abs(v) set to 0. No sin(v). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 46:** `cos(c6*v + c7*exp(c8*x))` — x-dependent phase. Cannot reduce to sin(v). **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 47:** Set c1=0, c8=0. Has sin. **MATCH**

**Candidate 48:** `c6*x**c7*sin(c8*v+c9)` — Set c7=0 gives c6*sin(c8*v+c9). Set c1=0, c5=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 49:** Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 50:** `c4*cos(c5+v)` — c5 is free, equivalent to cos(v+c5) = sin(v) with c5=-π/2. **MATCH**

**Candidate 51:** Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 52:** Set c7=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 53:** `c5*Max(0,c6-v)` — Set c5=0. Set c1=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 54:** `c6*log(c7*exp(c8*x+c9*v)+1)` — Softplus, not reducible. Set c6=0. Then c1*v**3, c2*v**5 set to 0. No sin(v). **NO MATCH**
